Jquery

<span data-key="a0ee5eea5643463d98a97f3072210b59"><span data-offset-key="a0ee5eea5643463d98a97f3072210b59:0">Selecting Elements with jQuery</span></span>

<span data-key="5b6358e0b85a4c32a53d4cdba308ff86"><span data-offset-key="5b6358e0b85a4c32a53d4cdba308ff86:0">JavaScript is most commonly used to get or modify the content or value of the HTML elements on the page, as well as to apply some effects like show, hide, animations etc. But, before you can perform any action you need to find or select the target HTML element.</span></span>

<span data-key="071870758210453f8e7df62e0a80dd66"><span data-offset-key="071870758210453f8e7df62e0a80dd66:0">Selecting the elements through a typical JavaScript approach could be very painful, but the jQuery works like a magic here. The ability of making the DOM elements selection simple and easy is one of the most powerful feature of the jQuery.</span></span>

<span data-key="2bbc43162ff648588e5a61b00774880f">**Tip:**<span data-offset-key="2bbc43162ff648588e5a61b00774880f:1"> The jQuery supports almost all the </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-tutorial/css-selectors.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="79f143167fbf42d98dee1e55bf25704f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="75b0ebef90cf48e6b8d810dbfe531bd9"><span data-offset-key="75b0ebef90cf48e6b8d810dbfe531bd9:0">selectors</span></span></span></a><span data-key="296a4b02529b4b1c9d8fb66e858461fa"><span data-offset-key="296a4b02529b4b1c9d8fb66e858461fa:0"> defined in the latest CSS3 specifications, as well as it has its own custom selectors. These custom selectors greatly enhance the capabilities selecting the HTML elements on a page.</span></span>

<span data-key="45985db1e6b44e96aaf7e0aba6f58eec"><span data-offset-key="45985db1e6b44e96aaf7e0aba6f58eec:0">In the following sections, you will see some of the common ways of selecting the elements on a page and do something with them using the jQuery.</span></span>

<span data-key="2a272be7e48443899cb1cbe5f810d65e"><span data-offset-key="2a272be7e48443899cb1cbe5f810d65e:0">Selecting Elements by ID</span></span>

<span data-key="a6a638970b8443b3976716bedf579198"><span data-offset-key="a6a638970b8443b3976716bedf579198:0">You can use the ID selector to select a single element with the unique ID on the page.</span></span>

<span data-key="0701b31d1fc84615b6daebf660ac3a82"><span data-offset-key="0701b31d1fc84615b6daebf660ac3a82:0">For example, the following jQuery code will select and highlight an element having the ID attribute </span>`id="mark"`<span data-offset-key="0701b31d1fc84615b6daebf660ac3a82:2">, when the document is ready to be manipulated.</span></span>

<span data-key="34941381dd954233ac0045722b114548"><span data-offset-key="34941381dd954233ac0045722b114548:0">In the above example we've performed a simple jQuery operation by changing the color of the heading i.e. the </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/html-tutorial/html-headings.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="89233270a5704f829bbb08101d4b8aef" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="d9c804b2494c41898bf2f91c8c1a979d"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="d9c804b2494c41898bf2f91c8c1a979d:0">&lt;h1&gt;</code></span></span></a><span data-key="81eb9e4e866b4ba4b12c64c0d440e93a"><span data-offset-key="81eb9e4e866b4ba4b12c64c0d440e93a:0"> element using the jQuery element selector and </span>`css()`<span data-offset-key="81eb9e4e866b4ba4b12c64c0d440e93a:2"> method when the document is ready which is known as document ready event. We'll learn about jQuery selectors, events and methods in upcoming chapters.</span></span>

<span data-key="08eff4ed35384846b0f06d764ceceefc"><span data-offset-key="08eff4ed35384846b0f06d764ceceefc:0">jQuery Events</span></span>

<span data-key="9e65222b1a4845b881edb4a2d2c56355"><span data-offset-key="9e65222b1a4845b881edb4a2d2c56355:0">In this tutorial you will learn how to handle events with jQuery.</span></span>

<span data-key="6a2fd00e123744b6bcc2b94479b5a915"><span data-offset-key="6a2fd00e123744b6bcc2b94479b5a915:0">What are Events</span></span>

<span data-key="17d6e0c5079d4c31a92bd319b1bd1481"><span data-offset-key="17d6e0c5079d4c31a92bd319b1bd1481:0">Events are often triggered by the user's interaction with the web page, such as when a link or button is clicked, text is entered into an input box or textarea, selection is made in a select box, key is pressed on the keyboard, the mouse pointer is moved etc. In some cases, the Browser itself can trigger the events, such as the page load and unload events.</span></span>

<span data-key="dfeefbffe4674bb8bef53cd1a6ab2f03"><span data-offset-key="dfeefbffe4674bb8bef53cd1a6ab2f03:0">jQuery enhances the basic event-handling mechanisms by offering the events methods for most native browser events, some of these methods are </span>`ready()`<span data-offset-key="dfeefbffe4674bb8bef53cd1a6ab2f03:2">, </span>`click()`<span data-offset-key="dfeefbffe4674bb8bef53cd1a6ab2f03:4">, </span>`keypress()`<span data-offset-key="dfeefbffe4674bb8bef53cd1a6ab2f03:6">, </span>`focus()`<span data-offset-key="dfeefbffe4674bb8bef53cd1a6ab2f03:8">, </span>`blur()`<span data-offset-key="dfeefbffe4674bb8bef53cd1a6ab2f03:10">, </span>`change()`<span data-offset-key="dfeefbffe4674bb8bef53cd1a6ab2f03:12">, etc. For example, to execute some JavaScript code when the DOM is ready, you can use the jQuery </span>`ready()`<span data-offset-key="dfeefbffe4674bb8bef53cd1a6ab2f03:14"> method, like this:</span></span>

<span data-key="ee35f81038cc4f5c8c1badc132dc2068">**Example**</span>

<span data-key="2fd70c4b76df4b01b2871cccc1618d74"><span data-offset-key="2fd70c4b76df4b01b2871cccc1618d74:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/codelab.php?topic=jquery&amp;file=execute-a-function-once-the-page-dom-is-ready" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="feab098f385e4bf8b41192448517c0a2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="a691a06e5b5949458af6ab4806710b52"><span data-offset-key="a691a06e5b5949458af6ab4806710b52:0">Try this code Â»</span></span></span></a><span data-key="b0c66ebf040441c58ff6a4094eea96bd"><span data-offset-key="b0c66ebf040441c58ff6a4094eea96bd:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span data-key="0e1fb60b648c4bbc938196e43dc26da7">**Note:**<span data-offset-key="0e1fb60b648c4bbc938196e43dc26da7:1"> The </span>`$(document).ready()`<span data-offset-key="0e1fb60b648c4bbc938196e43dc26da7:3"> is an event that is used to manipulate a page safely with the jQuery. Code included inside this event will only run once the page DOM is ready i.e. when the document is ready to be manipulated.</span></span>

<span data-key="128e0367357f422ea2b9cce4b51b6ec1"><span data-offset-key="128e0367357f422ea2b9cce4b51b6ec1:0">In general, the events can be categorized into four main groups â€” </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/jquery-tutorial/jquery-events.php#mouse-events" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c7546f4df1cd42fb889cd78d3cbc3501" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="f3e48f308b2444efb1c346ad3894c746"><span data-offset-key="f3e48f308b2444efb1c346ad3894c746:0">mouse events</span></span></span></a><span data-key="db8e372d43984dd796038d283a87cbdf"><span data-offset-key="db8e372d43984dd796038d283a87cbdf:0">, </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/jquery-tutorial/jquery-events.php#keyboard-events" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="baa803ec524f483c85624a733ebb4278" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="2c773f6f0b414d1eb362b3f9643a20b2"><span data-offset-key="2c773f6f0b414d1eb362b3f9643a20b2:0">keyboard events</span></span></span></a><span data-key="ec6296d33924480982da4a2f30a42522"><span data-offset-key="ec6296d33924480982da4a2f30a42522:0">, </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/jquery-tutorial/jquery-events.php#form-events" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="52b9bb2258a5466cb2509fe7ec19924e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="2275eb2425b94849b65c03a437ef7ba6"><span data-offset-key="2275eb2425b94849b65c03a437ef7ba6:0">form events</span></span></span></a><span data-key="ebee7e37983e400b95c6dcb050164f27"><span data-offset-key="ebee7e37983e400b95c6dcb050164f27:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/jquery-tutorial/jquery-events.php#document-and-window-events" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9f735fba381f40a28e231c65a84b68ff" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="0d90e17d573844ea9f32563c25605037"><span data-offset-key="0d90e17d573844ea9f32563c25605037:0">document/window events</span></span></span></a><span data-key="c2f03f4165b249af9f8450d23af8e308"><span data-offset-key="c2f03f4165b249af9f8450d23af8e308:0">. The following section will give you the brief overview of all these events as well as related jQuery methods one by one.</span></span>

<span data-key="6bbf7347db1743b99218a0df02c6512f"><span data-offset-key="6bbf7347db1743b99218a0df02c6512f:0">Mouse Events</span></span>

<span data-key="fd74381897a647e1b186bc454bc922b2"><span data-offset-key="fd74381897a647e1b186bc454bc922b2:0">A mouse event is fired when the user click some element, move the mouse pointer etc. Here're some commonly used jQuery methods to handle the mouse events.</span></span>

<span data-key="d70c6c5fcb064cb1ba853a5dace52a1d"><span data-offset-key="d70c6c5fcb064cb1ba853a5dace52a1d:0">The </span>`click()`<span data-offset-key="d70c6c5fcb064cb1ba853a5dace52a1d:2"> Method</span></span>

<span data-key="b1fc1bcd289b4c0ab84068d7927bb0e6"><span data-offset-key="b1fc1bcd289b4c0ab84068d7927bb0e6:0">jQuery Show and Hide Effects</span></span>

<span data-key="0c006e12d5da4621978b7694452173b1"><span data-offset-key="0c006e12d5da4621978b7694452173b1:0">In this tutorial you will learn how to show hide HTML elements using jQuery.</span></span>

<span data-key="eb0cca8c48fb4fa1abbc76d81237626c"><span data-offset-key="eb0cca8c48fb4fa1abbc76d81237626c:0">The </span>`hide()`<span data-offset-key="eb0cca8c48fb4fa1abbc76d81237626c:2"> method simply sets the </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/html-tutorial/html-styles.php#inline-styles" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5d4b8f9d94d349d18d102b025c4c700e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="5758aaf3a5184c559944a463606db195"><span data-offset-key="5758aaf3a5184c559944a463606db195:0">inline style</span></span></span></a><span data-key="d4b95f8696a047e9a6252567a1ebb731"><span data-offset-key="d4b95f8696a047e9a6252567a1ebb731:0"> </span>`display: none`<span data-offset-key="d4b95f8696a047e9a6252567a1ebb731:2"> for the selected elements. Conversely, the </span>`show()`<span data-offset-key="d4b95f8696a047e9a6252567a1ebb731:4"> method restores the </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-tutorial/css-display.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d91ed291f1fd44fdb67f03dd31faed62" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="d0d7c41b04374d80b0a236a681f5369b"><span data-offset-key="d0d7c41b04374d80b0a236a681f5369b:0">display properties</span></span></span></a><span data-key="9c9e196f4ab2467dbb121f6756afe660"><span data-offset-key="9c9e196f4ab2467dbb121f6756afe660:0"> of the matched set of elements to whatever they initially wereâ€”typically block, inline, or inline-blockâ€”before the inline style </span>`display: none`<span data-offset-key="9c9e196f4ab2467dbb121f6756afe660:2"> was applied to them. Here's is an example.</span></span>

<span data-key="cb421f8c1eaf418e916d81a8c16c7805">**Example**</span>

<span data-key="680728e4ca7f438a94a7136d9643df3b"><span data-offset-key="680728e4ca7f438a94a7136d9643df3b:0">jQuery Fading Effects</span></span>

<span data-key="5dbdfbab08de478a92ae20fe8bb9e14e">**Note:**<span data-offset-key="5dbdfbab08de478a92ae20fe8bb9e14e:1"> The effect of </span>`fadeIn()`<span data-offset-key="5dbdfbab08de478a92ae20fe8bb9e14e:3">/</span>`fadeOut()`<span data-offset-key="5dbdfbab08de478a92ae20fe8bb9e14e:5"> method looks similar to </span>`show()`<span data-offset-key="5dbdfbab08de478a92ae20fe8bb9e14e:7">/</span>`hide()`<span data-offset-key="5dbdfbab08de478a92ae20fe8bb9e14e:9">, but unlike </span>`show()`<span data-offset-key="5dbdfbab08de478a92ae20fe8bb9e14e:11">/</span>`hide()`<span data-offset-key="5dbdfbab08de478a92ae20fe8bb9e14e:13"> method the </span>`fadeIn()`<span data-offset-key="5dbdfbab08de478a92ae20fe8bb9e14e:15">/</span>`fadeOut()`<span data-offset-key="5dbdfbab08de478a92ae20fe8bb9e14e:17"> method only animates the opacity of the target elements and does not animates their dimensions.</span></span>

<span data-key="6a52da859f5a4974b0b8341b1d340e0c"><span data-offset-key="6a52da859f5a4974b0b8341b1d340e0c:0">You can also specify a </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/jquery-tutorial/jquery-callback.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="381997fced0b473db062f24185a8b39f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="d9ef1941a11f4f6fb1a6b8ab9a1dc517"><span data-offset-key="d9ef1941a11f4f6fb1a6b8ab9a1dc517:0">callback function</span></span></span></a><span data-key="0b1f84b89c5d47c8b328570d3fa4de70"><span data-offset-key="0b1f84b89c5d47c8b328570d3fa4de70:0"> to be executed after the </span>`fadeIn()`<span data-offset-key="0b1f84b89c5d47c8b328570d3fa4de70:2"> or </span>`fadeOut()`<span data-offset-key="0b1f84b89c5d47c8b328570d3fa4de70:4"> method completes. We'll learn more about the callback function in upcoming chapters.</span></span>

<span data-key="91cf66f4bd5743dcbff039e0d2212f68"><span data-offset-key="91cf66f4bd5743dcbff039e0d2212f68:0">jQuery </span>`fadeTo()`<span data-offset-key="91cf66f4bd5743dcbff039e0d2212f68:2"> Method</span></span>

<span data-key="65ae64d85d8c4ef8b08df6c3911f2cd2"><span data-offset-key="65ae64d85d8c4ef8b08df6c3911f2cd2:0">The jQuery </span>`fadeTo()`<span data-offset-key="65ae64d85d8c4ef8b08df6c3911f2cd2:2"> method is similar to the </span>`.fadeIn()`<span data-offset-key="65ae64d85d8c4ef8b08df6c3911f2cd2:4"> method, but unlike </span>`.fadeIn()`<span data-offset-key="65ae64d85d8c4ef8b08df6c3911f2cd2:6"> the </span>`fadeTo()`<span data-offset-key="65ae64d85d8c4ef8b08df6c3911f2cd2:8"> method lets you fade in the elements to a certain opacity level.$(selector).fadeTo(speed, opacity, callback);</span></span>

<span data-key="0662cfd9b7b44361ac711e698e16e85a"><span data-offset-key="0662cfd9b7b44361ac711e698e16e85a:0">The required opacity parameter specifies the final opacity of the target elements that can be a number between 0 and 1. The duration or speed parameter is also required for this method that specifies the duration of the fade to animation.</span></span>

<span data-key="95dc71b09bbd4b2b86e41c21beab21f2">**Example**</span>

<span data-key="082aed6178e3425298253f10a8b045d3"><span data-offset-key="082aed6178e3425298253f10a8b045d3:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/codelab.php?topic=jquery&amp;file=fade-to-effect" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d34c6edc0f164cbe98c937aaa7a13968" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="211f423691fb4d66ab1fcac4574433ed"><span data-offset-key="211f423691fb4d66ab1fcac4574433ed:0">Try this code Â»</span></span></span></a><span data-key="afbb0c209f2040838848633ee80acc3f"><span data-offset-key="afbb0c209f2040838848633ee80acc3f:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span data-key="cd046d04fde74ee6a97110e8a7ef420f"><span data-offset-key="cd046d04fde74ee6a97110e8a7ef420f:0">jQuery Sliding Effects</span></span>

<span data-key="89ba89bf165844f5a41e0030ab4715d8"><span data-offset-key="89ba89bf165844f5a41e0030ab4715d8:0">In this tutorial you will learn how to create slide motion effect using jQuery.</span></span>

<span data-key="ddaedeba28ba488db40bf12817d70b1f"><span data-offset-key="ddaedeba28ba488db40bf12817d70b1f:0">jQuery </span>`slideUp()`<span data-offset-key="ddaedeba28ba488db40bf12817d70b1f:2"> and </span>`slideDown()`<span data-offset-key="ddaedeba28ba488db40bf12817d70b1f:4"> Methods</span></span>

<span data-key="96f753503ce441a8ad8cd4f9454f036f"><span data-offset-key="96f753503ce441a8ad8cd4f9454f036f:0">The jQuery </span>`slideUp()`<span data-offset-key="96f753503ce441a8ad8cd4f9454f036f:2"> and </span>`slideDown()`<span data-offset-key="96f753503ce441a8ad8cd4f9454f036f:4"> methods is used to hide or show the HTML elements by gradually decreasing or increasing their height (i.e. by sliding them up or down).</span></span>

<span data-key="50ad663f7ee1468f9efb931946cadb52">**Example**</span>

<span data-key="fb0437f0f077444680cf77d712bb6b08"><span data-offset-key="fb0437f0f077444680cf77d712bb6b08:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/codelab.php?topic=jquery&amp;file=slide-up-and-down-effects" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="19188727e0bd4c5780d9aa32c69a43c0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="d006ff8e14264bc282015e672d28376a"><span data-offset-key="d006ff8e14264bc282015e672d28376a:0">Try this code Â»</span></span></span></a><span data-key="f12f9d8401ee4d868029e37d8142cca7"><span data-offset-key="f12f9d8401ee4d868029e37d8142cca7:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="03e400f7230740bfa7547fcda7b8893a"><span data-offset-key="03e400f7230740bfa7547fcda7b8893a:0">Like other jQuery effects methods, you can optionally specify the duration or speed parameter for the </span>`slideUp()`<span data-offset-key="03e400f7230740bfa7547fcda7b8893a:2"> and </span>`slideDown()`<span data-offset-key="03e400f7230740bfa7547fcda7b8893a:4"> methods to control how long the slide animation will run. <span data-key="c20c1c3bd3de49a3ae38bd66a8c5e719"><span data-offset-key="c20c1c3bd3de49a3ae38bd66a8c5e719:0">The jQuery </span>`slideToggle()`<span data-offset-key="c20c1c3bd3de49a3ae38bd66a8c5e719:2"> method show or hide the selected elements by animating their height in such a way that if the element is initially displayed, it will be slide up; if hidden, it will be slide down i.e. toggles between the </span>`slideUp()`<span data-offset-key="c20c1c3bd3de49a3ae38bd66a8c5e719:4"> and </span>`slideDown()`<span data-offset-key="c20c1c3bd3de49a3ae38bd66a8c5e719:6"> methods.</span></span>

<span data-key="20d90a2b15774748971bba3051363a3c"><span data-offset-key="20d90a2b15774748971bba3051363a3c:0"> // Code to be executed</span></span>

7

<span data-key="56617acd102248d19c61bb7c3850e7e8"><span data-offset-key="56617acd102248d19c61bb7c3850e7e8:0"> alert("The slide-toggle effect is completed.");</span></span>

8

<span data-key="b9437342f924479d9f60613974418b6e"><span data-offset-key="b9437342f924479d9f60613974418b6e:0"> });</span></span>

9

<span data-key="cdc55d0fdb8a48fda375dbf5ee98d7c8"><span data-offset-key="cdc55d0fdb8a48fda375dbf5ee98d7c8:0"> });</span></span>

10

<span data-key="8efe3b23d5674449b822eff60290a36c"><span data-offset-key="8efe3b23d5674449b822eff60290a36c:0">});</span></span>

11

<span data-key="9344d99580454a419fce44c3cb1d0235"><span data-offset-key="9344d99580454a419fce44c3cb1d0235:0">&lt;/script&gt;</span></span>

Copied!

<span data-key="534027c14aa34e99bc0d618f329b923a"><span data-offset-key="534027c14aa34e99bc0d618f329b923a:0">jQuery Animation Effects</span></span>

<span data-key="65f3c12330bf4616928df9f4a83b7358"><span data-offset-key="65f3c12330bf4616928df9f4a83b7358:0">In this tutorial you will learn how to animate CSS properties using jQuery.</span></span>

<span data-key="cac7a22177b3453e91c8df7b3ca335df"><span data-offset-key="cac7a22177b3453e91c8df7b3ca335df:0">jQuery </span>`animate()`<span data-offset-key="cac7a22177b3453e91c8df7b3ca335df:2"> Method</span></span>

<span data-key="ce5e21a0411f4fea978be88eb6b75087"><span data-offset-key="ce5e21a0411f4fea978be88eb6b75087:0">The jQuery </span>`animate()`<span data-offset-key="ce5e21a0411f4fea978be88eb6b75087:2"> method is used to create custom animations. The </span>`animate()`<span data-offset-key="ce5e21a0411f4fea978be88eb6b75087:4"> method is typically used to animate numeric CSS properties, for example, </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-reference/css-width-property.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="318762b3dca94ed8a470ef25a08b5c98" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="887d396e6e0b4eae800f8ba0842c835f"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="887d396e6e0b4eae800f8ba0842c835f:0">width</code></span></span></a><span data-key="0b17645bf1bd4ddcbe2120f270eee650"><span data-offset-key="0b17645bf1bd4ddcbe2120f270eee650:0">, </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-reference/css-height-property.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="dc7c03d8311940b9a334945ca2f0f85e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="e0cc42318e3c42af8ae0bc961282d510"><code data-key="9411e0f844f24993af9772db8ab06e14"><span data-offset-key="9411e0f844f24993af9772db8ab06e14:0">, </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-reference/css-margin-property.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="05f22efca6b54eb595c8a853dc6b023e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="eb97e500cce04bafbb9a641acc57d4ad"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="eb97e500cce04bafbb9a641acc57d4ad:0">margin</code></span></span></a><span data-key="79caa0172c6b450eb21a28ad7ba69fd8"><span data-offset-key="79caa0172c6b450eb21a28ad7ba69fd8:0">, </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-reference/css-padding-property.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4641f9d79134452a9767e53b1e048151" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="c651da8a9dec4db7a4431127cdaa76b4"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="c651da8a9dec4db7a4431127cdaa76b4:0">padding</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8ef686777c6d44c3ad68e910f08323a3"><span data-offset-key="8ef686777c6d44c3ad68e910f08323a3:0">, </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-reference/css-opacity-property.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9ff80919a25f42f7a3deffa928841074" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="186d2f632bba41ffb4896499ca231cfe"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="186d2f632bba41ffb4896499ca231cfe:0">opacity</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9897eb19db534fc3ab26221abd135e3d"><span data-offset-key="9897eb19db534fc3ab26221abd135e3d:0">, </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-reference/css-top-property.php" data-key="6263777ad9b449e0a077565979a65f0d"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="6263777ad9b449e0a077565979a65f0d:0">top</code></span></span></a><span data-key="0371bf98556f4c57a56c79ebc56b6e4f"><span data-offset-key="0371bf98556f4c57a56c79ebc56b6e4f:0">, </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-reference/css-left-property.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1d84f57e716b497f9c7230d415455b35" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="b3d66c5449c64be69d6af92a0e7ec7a8"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t data-offset-key="2fad67b2c16a40b6829dea1b4cc3ac14:0">, etc. but the non-numeric properties such as </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-reference/css-color-property.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ab731b64732d4318a647bb34921c0b5f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="afbd75ccbab34facbbb17799e41eea0b"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="afbd75ccbab34facbbb17799e41eea0b:0">color</code></span></span></a><span data-key="aca99ddb6aa24946bb0602987247d747"><span data-offset-key="aca99ddb6aa24946bb0602987247d747:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-reference/css-background-color-property.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a7996f71475143078341f7ed55613b82" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="4ddaadd13c4c48a0afae91cf1ee637da"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t data-offset-key="3f2f48d36b3844f99adeb4904adbb150:0"> cannot be animated using the basic jQuery functionality.</span></span>

<span data-key="72a9b0fe9c44436b9e7e3983ab8c07bb">**Note:**<span data-offset-key="72a9b0fe9c44436b9e7e3983ab8c07bb:1"> Not all CSS properties are animatable. In general, any CSS property that accepts values that are numbers, lengths, percentages, or colors is animatable. However, the color animation is not support by the core jQuery library. To manipulate and animate the color use the </span></span><a href="https://github.com/jquery/jquery-color" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="edc047c5d1c14d0899c0b8e07ad88c5e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="5467cd2ade104a95bea23b26fcc8ed22"><span data-offset-key="5467cd2ade104a95bea23b26fcc8ed22:0">jQuery color plugin</span></span></span></a><span data-key="4979c4def8c045aeac47ff453ab1de88"><span data-offset-key="4979c4def8c045aeac47ff453ab1de88:0">.</span></span>

<span data-key="9947a30d7a414989a8fd849e120eb666"><span data-offset-key="9947a30d7a414989a8fd849e120eb666:0">Syntax</span></span>

<span data-key="83afcbaacd9749d9b4b44c53a0848343"><span data-offset-key="83afcbaacd9749d9b4b44c53a0848343:0">The basic syntax of the jQuery </span>`animate()`<span data-offset-key="83afcbaacd9749d9b4b44c53a0848343:2"> method can be given with:$(selector).animate({ properties }, duration, callback);</span></span>

<span data-key="4bfa457a9b3143b4b3a8442a07cd5ee5"><span data-offset-key="4bfa457a9b3143b4b3a8442a07cd5ee5:0">The parameters of the </span>`animate()`<span data-offset-key="4bfa457a9b3143b4b3a8442a07cd5ee5:2"> method have the following meanings:</span></span>

- <span data-key="39dc88b26b094243adc9668cd6546569"><span data-offset-key="39dc88b26b094243adc9668cd6546569:0">The required properties parameter defines the </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-reference/css3-properties.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="42087f6f7e81435a8b80a19b251e702b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="266bedcf4c67450c8271f9edc8f98f75"><span data-offset-key="266bedcf4c67450c8271f9edc8f98f75:0">CSS properties</span></span></span></a><span data-key="d35277d9c9494fc79bd786846d274b40"><span data-offset-key="d35277d9c9494fc79bd786846d274b40:0"> to be animated.</span></span>

- <span data-key="5687f61dc6664cef88b3ab5b000aee35"><span data-offset-key="5687f61dc6664cef88b3ab5b000aee35:0">The optional duration parameter specifies how long the animation will run. Durations can be specified either using one of the predefined string </span>`'slow'`<span data-offset-key="5687f61dc6664cef88b3ab5b000aee35:2"> or </span>`'fast'`<span data-offset-key="5687f61dc6664cef88b3ab5b000aee35:4">, or in a number of milliseconds; higher values indicate slower animations.</span></span>

- <span data-key="9728fa45a0214004be1ae2053d40ce12"><span data-offset-key="9728fa45a0214004be1ae2053d40ce12:0">The optional </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/jquery-tutorial/jquery-callback.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f799723a16444f9c893acaa8c5e8eba9" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="7fa7cc6fece24c88b3b59749e3edef52"><span data-offset-key="7fa7cc6fece24c88b3b59749e3edef52:0">callback</span></span></span></a><span data-key="93cf8e5bb9f04ab0834a5dd1750a2400"><span data-offset-key="93cf8e5bb9f04ab0834a5dd1750a2400:0"> parameter is a function to call once the animation is complete.</span></span>

<span data-key="cb0b82efde1942399c704fed54d3a01d"><span data-offset-key="cb0b82efde1942399c704fed54d3a01d:0">Here's a simple example of the jQuery </span>`animate()`<span data-offset-key="cb0b82efde1942399c704fed54d3a01d:2"> method that animates an image from its original position to the right by 300 pixels on click of the button.</span></span>

<span data-key="4988b0d32f454407b91a2b09aae3b75b">**Note:**<span data-offset-key="4988b0d32f454407b91a2b09aae3b75b:1"> All HTML elements have static position by default. Since the static element cannot be moved, so you must set the CSS </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-reference/css-position-property.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a380ea90947841ecb68c52d5ab12b5dd" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="dba5559f4abc47019802575ab3ffce4d"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="dba5559f4abc47019802575ab3ffce4d:0">position</code></span></span></a><span data-key="40967f85a5624d7685e3045d309844d2"><span data-offset-key="40967f85a5624d7685e3045d309844d2:0"> property for the element to </span>`relative`<span data-offset-key="40967f85a5624d7685e3045d309844d2:2">, </span>`fixed`<span data-offset-key="40967f85a5624d7685e3045d309844d2:4">, or </span>`absolute`<span data-offset-key="40967f85a5624d7685e3045d309844d2:6"> to manipulate or animate its position.</span></span>

<span data-key="c4463bf1c76d4d7e8ae5b00af26f0899"><span data-offset-key="c4463bf1c76d4d7e8ae5b00af26f0899:0">Animate Multiple Properties At Once</span></span>

<span data-key="fd36676f129b4ad7857426449d28bffa"><span data-offset-key="fd36676f129b4ad7857426449d28bffa:0">You can also animate multiple properties of an element together at the same time using the </span>`animate()`<span data-offset-key="fd36676f129b4ad7857426449d28bffa:2"> method. All the properties animated simultaneously without any delay.</span></span>

<span data-key="4dbddc9bbc10420286237b29ec3e18cd">**Example**</span>

<span data-key="fd8b21c622eb41b7bc2c3f43783fbd81">**Note:**<span data-offset-key="fd8b21c622eb41b7bc2c3f43783fbd81:1"> The </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-reference/css3-properties.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="173eab64a5c34282a9df5af3bd31e2b4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="573c34bd59794573aabcecb85a6379df"><span data-offset-key="573c34bd59794573aabcecb85a6379df:0">CSS properties</span></span></span></a><span data-key="46a2299634a3484c9a69b55515ee4c58"><span data-offset-key="46a2299634a3484c9a69b55515ee4c58:0"> names must be camel-cased when using with the </span>`animate()`<span data-offset-key="46a2299634a3484c9a69b55515ee4c58:2"> method, e.g. if you want to animate the font size you need to write </span>`'fontSize'`<span data-offset-key="46a2299634a3484c9a69b55515ee4c58:4"> rather than </span>`'`</span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-reference/css-font-size-property.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="501cbc30a2f74c2eafb3dd6ff6d0fffd" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="8ae815e15d5e46d0a4bb387ef3e0d7d5"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="8ae815e15d5e46d0a4bb387ef3e0d7d5:0">font-size</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ca747eb25c4e4b2d937d439335fed9e6">`'`<span data-offset-key="ca747eb25c4e4b2d937d439335fed9e6:1">. Similarly, write </span>`'marginLeft'`<span data-offset-key="ca747eb25c4e4b2d937d439335fed9e6:3"> instead of </span>`'`</span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-reference/css-margin-left-property.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e79edcdeb8b24ca8ac64741f068cb366" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="5d6a528920ee49c38763fe3889d781a1"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="5d6a528920ee49c38763fe3889d781a1:0">margin-left</code></span></span></a><span data-key="229f614bb4544542817c3c43e13f8f15">`'`<span data-offset-key="229f614bb4544542817c3c43e13f8f15:1">, </span>`'borderWidth'`<span data-offset-key="229f614bb4544542817c3c43e13f8f15:3"> instead of </span>`'`</span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-reference/css-border-width-property.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="170dcd50a218424ab7a0f05f82005faf" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="c2028f83c31548589231e12aaa90cb08"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="c2028f83c31548589231e12aaa90cb08:0">border-width</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d0e1f2ac3758427aa89c1eef0813974a">`'`<span data-offset-key="d0e1f2ac3758427aa89c1eef0813974a:1">, and so on.</span></span>

<span data-key="4b13d35d7482467cafae7e57bb76fd2e">**Tip:**<span data-offset-key="4b13d35d7482467cafae7e57bb76fd2e:1"> You must set the </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-reference/css-border-style-property.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bdaf9ac4fefb448d9091a8beed0499e8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="87481050267c4267b752770f2229dfd4"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="87481050267c4267b752770f2229dfd4:0">border-style</code></span></span></a><span data-key="49baa984de2e412ebca6e34b3b728b2c"><span data-offset-key="49baa984de2e412ebca6e34b3b728b2c:0"> property for the element before animating its </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-reference/css-border-width-property.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3052aa37d55642e8a79d51feb5ac419b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="7ecf5f0bbd5c4ea39c808eb0f299f902"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="7ecf5f0bbd5c4ea39c808eb0f299f902:0">border-width</code></span></span></a><span data-key="7f19486ed69e46898c1881363a0d1bb5"><span data-offset-key="7f19486ed69e46898c1881363a0d1bb5:0"> property. <span data-key="44cf9ffc36b14d84a11ce186440affcb"><span data-offset-key="44cf9ffc36b14d84a11ce186440affcb:0">Animate Multiple Properties One by One or Queued Animations</span></span>

<span data-key="da093700940c41adbe6d16bc5af394d7"><span data-offset-key="da093700940c41adbe6d16bc5af394d7:0">jQuery Chaining</span></span>

<span data-key="38eb9d8360014ba5a4e92ed38d8de252"><span data-offset-key="38eb9d8360014ba5a4e92ed38d8de252:0">In this tutorial you will learn how chain multiple methods in jQuery.</span></span>

<span data-key="e16887eb157e4c1b8420e0e8caa5c43b"><span data-offset-key="e16887eb157e4c1b8420e0e8caa5c43b:0">jQuery Method Chaining</span></span>

<span data-key="d0584bd268d646a4bd11e243b892ca79"><span data-offset-key="d0584bd268d646a4bd11e243b892ca79:0">The jQuery provides another robust feature called method chaining that allows us to perform multiple action on the same set of elements, all within a single line of code.</span></span>

<span data-key="e17740d5cfeb4ee18286a2dba568c156"><span data-offset-key="e17740d5cfeb4ee18286a2dba568c156:0">This is possible because most of the jQuery methods return a jQuery object that can be further used to call another method. Here's an example.</span></span>

<span data-key="1475c27599bd45ecb06dea3c96efa05d"><span data-offset-key="1475c27599bd45ecb06dea3c96efa05d:0">The above example demonstrate the chaining of three </span>`animate()`<span data-offset-key="1475c27599bd45ecb06dea3c96efa05d:2"> method. When a user click the trigger button, it expands the </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/html-reference/html-p-tag.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9e1c83f8d3dc4a74b9057381060cb792" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="79759e6e21a54a48a7c1ee4149d1148f"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="79759e6e21a54a48a7c1ee4149d1148f:0">&lt;p&gt;</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e33287d0a8c64038afd97c5a211bad3b"><span data-offset-key="e33287d0a8c64038afd97c5a211bad3b:0"> to 100% width. Once the </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-reference/css-width-property.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a2b3374d6b064e339435dea70aaa1af3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="f966ed9b90304db0a5bfa348c043fb41"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="f966ed9b90304db0a5bfa348c043fb41:0">width</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e8d64bae2a724454b03e55b0166667a6"><span data-offset-key="e8d64bae2a724454b03e55b0166667a6:0"> change is complete the </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-reference/css-font-size-property.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="29a8cac861204b25a22f3202bbbc9477" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="f38a180fcbe647bbb02c5469af4942ac"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="f38a180fcbe647bbb02c5469af4942ac:0">font-size</code></span></span></a><span data-key="92f54f1e94ed43a4ba668002aba23d14"><span data-offset-key="92f54f1e94ed43a4ba668002aba23d14:0"> is start animating and after its completion, the </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/css-reference/css-border-property.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="793902bdac6647ddba4488369ce91023" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="b96ccebbf76f48a087efaa3af60dc67b"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="b96ccebbf76f48a087efaa3af60dc67b:0">border</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8b133e472ebc48aa9a6d6fb20600a92f"><span data-offset-key="8b133e472ebc48aa9a6d6fb20600a92f:0"> animation will begin.</span></span>

<span data-key="3aa27813366345f1beb74bf5af432645">**Tip:**<span data-offset-key="3aa27813366345f1beb74bf5af432645:1"> The method chaining not only helps you to keep your jQuery code concise, but it also can improve your script's performance since browser doesn't have to find the same elements multiple times to do something with them.</span></span>

<span data-key="70f2946d08db48d6bfe67afb2ec5498e"><span data-offset-key="70f2946d08db48d6bfe67afb2ec5498e:0">You can also break a single line of code into multiple lines for greater readability. For example, the sequence of methods in the above example could also be written as:</span></span>

<span data-key="4203f55af9b84e28be2b6dffd6e68fa3"><span data-offset-key="4203f55af9b84e28be2b6dffd6e68fa3:0">Some jQuery methods doesn't return the jQuery object. In general, </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/jquery-tutorial/jquery-getter-and-setter.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8e5b978811e347c182443df0d68ff587" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="f5f2f5ba81f74127a0680298799899d8"><span data-offset-key="f5f2f5ba81f74127a0680298799899d8:0">setters</span></span></span></a><span data-key="a8d158735d9045c5a70679ca486dad06"><span data-offset-key="a8d158735d9045c5a70679ca486dad06:0"> i.e. methods that assign some value on a selection return a jQuery object, that allows you to continue calling jQuery methods on your selection. Whereas, </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/jquery-tutorial/jquery-getter-and-setter.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d945ca7702c3494cadc65f7730c8b291" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="1586f0c4c28442e48a40ddf3d0bb9f0c"><span data-offset-key="1586f0c4c28442e48a40ddf3d0bb9f0c:0">getters</span></span></span></a><span data-key="e7d3dc29c4aa4e6f83206dd1a2e332cf"><span data-offset-key="e7d3dc29c4aa4e6f83206dd1a2e332cf:0"> return the requested value, so you can't continue to call jQuery methods on the value returned by the getter.</span></span>

<span data-key="0567949ac15c43ee99b666f14faaf883"><span data-offset-key="0567949ac15c43ee99b666f14faaf883:0">A typical example of this scenario is the </span>`html()`<span data-offset-key="0567949ac15c43ee99b666f14faaf883:2"> method. If no parameters are passed to it, the HTML contents of the selected element is returned instead of a jQuery object.</span></span>

<span data-key="5f323799232a494fbaf8bf7f4b1db71b">**Example**</span>

<span data-key="fe90b24eb60749a49710bde472f78950"><span data-offset-key="fe90b24eb60749a49710bde472f78950:0">jQuery Callback</span></span>

<span data-key="a2a2a962ebf54904a431ecb3edb034e6"><span data-offset-key="a2a2a962ebf54904a431ecb3edb034e6:0">In this tutorial you will learn how define a callback function for the jQuery effect.</span></span>

<span data-key="c187fc656f03416c940ee715119ef8f1"><span data-offset-key="c187fc656f03416c940ee715119ef8f1:0">jQuery Callback Functions</span></span>

<span data-key="e0348fa192a644a49d95eb05a5b48785"><span data-offset-key="e0348fa192a644a49d95eb05a5b48785:0">JavaScript statements are executed line by line. But, since jQuery effect takes some time to finish the next line code may execute while the previous effect is still running. To prevent this from happening jQuery provides a callback function for each effect method.</span></span>

<span data-key="49788081b0754dabb238c3c2206d8384"><span data-offset-key="49788081b0754dabb238c3c2206d8384:0">A callback function is a function that is executed once the effect is complete. The callback function is passed as an argument to the effect methods and they typically appear as the last argument of the method. For example, the basic syntax of the jQuery </span>`slideToggle()`<span data-offset-key="49788081b0754dabb238c3c2206d8384:2"> effect method with a callback function can be given with:$(selector).slideToggle(duration, callback);</span></span>

<span data-key="c5c3e69302ed4bd0b06199145214d44e"><span data-offset-key="c5c3e69302ed4bd0b06199145214d44e:0">Consider the following example in which we've placed the </span>`slideToggle()`<span data-offset-key="c5c3e69302ed4bd0b06199145214d44e:2"> and </span>`alert()`<span data-offset-key="c5c3e69302ed4bd0b06199145214d44e:4"> statements next to each other. If you try this code the alert will be displayed immediately once you click the trigger button without waiting for slide toggle effect to complete.</span></span>

<span data-key="e1e736d66fc3446597b69f7ab1f8db2c">**Example**</span>

<span data-key="fd104ee5e9c149ff867e0d35f0aa4a97"><span data-offset-key="fd104ee5e9c149ff867e0d35f0aa4a97:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/codelab.php?topic=jquery&amp;file=method-without-callback" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="87b29936cb984599a24df681afca71f5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="7db6528eaa5c404eb949225232052b86"><span data-offset-key="7db6528eaa5c404eb949225232052b86:0">Try this code Â»</span></span></span></a><span data-key="1090bcbdbf5a459e8d6c70cbd4ae9c83"><span data-offset-key="1090bcbdbf5a459e8d6c70cbd4ae9c83:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

1

Copied!

<span data-key="cd38106708514131a9452f044e029e3c"><span data-offset-key="cd38106708514131a9452f044e029e3c:0">And, here's the modified version of the pevious example in which we've placed the </span>`alert()`<span data-offset-key="cd38106708514131a9452f044e029e3c:2"> statement inside a callback function for the </span>`slideToggle()`<span data-offset-key="cd38106708514131a9452f044e029e3c:4"> method. <span data-key="cf94d6a753ab4ab1a06fc5366d771e6a"><span data-offset-key="cf94d6a753ab4ab1a06fc5366d771e6a:0">Similarly, you can define the callback functions for the other jQuery effect methods, like </span>`show()`<span data-offset-key="cf94d6a753ab4ab1a06fc5366d771e6a:2">, </span>`hide()`<span data-offset-key="cf94d6a753ab4ab1a06fc5366d771e6a:4">, </span>`fadeIn()`<span data-offset-key="cf94d6a753ab4ab1a06fc5366d771e6a:6">, </span>`fadeOut()`<span data-offset-key="cf94d6a753ab4ab1a06fc5366d771e6a:8">, </span>`animate()`<span data-offset-key="cf94d6a753ab4ab1a06fc5366d771e6a:10">, etc.</span></span>

<span data-key="c1a20f058d2e4f2ca7d7117952d03ba0">**Note:**<span data-offset-key="c1a20f058d2e4f2ca7d7117952d03ba0:1"> If the effect method is applied to multiple elements, then the callback function is executed once for each selected element, not once for all.</span></span>

<span data-key="0c2b2cf1e8db43b8be96aae8ff28a2d5">**Example**</span>

<span data-key="a4bf128517f94c97a401f8331a5bd8cc"><span data-offset-key="a4bf128517f94c97a401f8331a5bd8cc:0">If you try the above example code, it will display the same alert message two times once per </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/html-reference/html-headings-tag.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="749a622666334578ae89476ec49ad856" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="d3f5b0d5220e42d785f61bb6091b1e14"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="d3f5b0d5220e42d785f61bb6091b1e14:0">&lt;h1&gt;</code></span></span></a><span data-key="3d01f5d4ab6944d99256d6de006c9f01"><span data-offset-key="3d01f5d4ab6944d99256d6de006c9f01:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://www.tutorialrepublic.com/html-reference/html-p-tag.php" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="88d6d11f214249ef81141d7abc9a097a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-5896_262-5897-240__"><span data-key="4d393d3f844446c1bfd8f3480aafe527"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="4d393d3f844446c1bfd8f3480aafe527:0">&lt;p&gt;</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d5c06fc7e5df4c02a1a58f1831932454"><span data-offset-key="d5c06fc7e5df4c02a1a58f1831932454:0"> element, upon clicking the trigger button.</span></span>
